,f.book_unit_no_name,f.book_unit_no_code FROM trans_jbooks a LEFT JOIN erp_fs_ngg.lib_erp_chart b ON b.account_id = a.account_id LEFT JOIN erp_fs_ngg.lib_erp_project c ON c.project_id = a.project_id LEFT JOIN erp_fs_ngg.lib_erp_department d ON d.department_id = a.department_id LEFT JOIN erp_fs_ngg.lib_erp_currency e ON e.currency_id = a.currency_id LEFT JOIN erp_fs_ngg.lib_erp_book_unit_no f ON f.book_unit_no_id = a.book_unit_no_id LEFT JOIN erp_fs_ngg.lib_erp_project_unit_no z ON z.project_unit_no_id = a.project_unit_no_id WHERE a.trans_id = 30 AND b.validation = 2 GROUP BY a.account_id,a.project_id,a.department_id,a.book_unit_no_id,z.project_unit_no_names ORDER BY account_code ASC
